<rating>5</rating><review>Tried Magic Kingdom and Sky Odyssey as a group of 3. Magic Kingdom was simple, whimsical, and fun, without being too short. Very kid-friendly.

Sky Odyssey was right up my alley, but not for everyone‚ÄîYou're exposed to a lot pretty early on, so you have to stay focused on what you actually need, what you can do, and what you've already done at any given point. It would have helped us to have 5 or more people in our group.

Our gamemaster Will was very experienced and enthusiastic. He gave us bonus time at the end of Sky Odyssey to solve the puzzles we didn't solve (84 minutes total), and he was still willing to answer all of our questions afterwards.

Other notes:
-The lobby looks a little run down, but the rooms are well decorated.
-Don't watch the lobby TV unless you're okay with some spoilers.
-The parking lot says 1 hour parking, but a member of our group parked there all night and had no problem. He did move his car once. Parking on Vermont is only safe after 7pm for weekdays.< /review>< pictures>

<name>Jem Cannu<//name></record></dataset><record>
< text>
We have been doing quite a lot of escape rooms over the past few months, so by this point I figured I had seen it all. Then Maze Escape rooms blew us away with Magic Kingdom, and I feel like I experience a new take on rooms that I highly recommend to both new players, and veterans alike. If you are experienced, don't expect a challenge, just enjoy the presentation and fact that you won't have to open a single lock, use a single key, or find any combinations. Every clue you solve is done through  the use of the "Magic" (aka technology) in the rooms. Definitely bring kids as its geared towards them more.

We also stuck around and did a second run on Secret Mission, as we were really happy with Magic Kingdom. While the theme and some puzzles were cool, overall it didn't feel quite as cohesive to us. We did bring a kid (who was there for Magic Kingdom but stuck around with us), and another person who was experience escape rooms for the first time, but the other 4 of us have done around 8 different rooms by now. This was the second time we ever came close to failing, with the last time being the first game we ever attempted. The biggest hurdle I think came from us discovering a clue earlier than we were supposed to, which caused us to trigger a really cool event at the same time as we were trying to solve that puzzle, leading us to think it was already resolved when in fact it wasn't. After the game, when it was explained to us, it all made sense logically, but in the moment it tripped us up and caused us to lose quite a bit of time. This was also one of the first games where a puzzle was solved by doing seemingly unrelated (but clearly related in hindsight) puzzles that had gated us from progressing in the puzzles. I don't think this is entirely the fault of the game, because as a whole the experience was totally positive, but we went from solving rooms with 10-20 minutes left to getting out with 2 minutes left!

That being said, we are super excited to come back and try Lunar Mission in the future, the staff was engaged and helpful and the fact you get to wear costume pieces to enhance the experience was very cool.<//text>

We arrived at the venue and the registration was really brief and there was a cool back-story to the task which gave it a little more meaning. The room was really well laid out and really immersed you in what you were doing. It took us a little while to getting going but when we did it was awesome! When we come back to LA we'll definitely do the other room. It was great!<//Review>

<UserId.>110640756616936456746<//UserId.><name>Sarah Zhang<//name><time>1459197155127</time><Rate>5<//Rate>< review>
LUNAR STATION is the one!

In short words:
The most impressive, innovative escape game in LA, with production value as good as Disneyland. This is a MUST TRY.

In long words:
If you think of first generation of escape game (locks and keys, paper hidden under the drawer) as parks near your home; most other escape games (some mechanic gadgets but still classic puzzles) as carnival; THE LUNER STATION is Hollywood studio!

We came here on the second day of opening. before game starts, we got our gears - astronauts' outfit, backpack and a black box to secure the tube. Then we split up into 2 teams. As we only have 2 players, one got stuck in the moon station and one came as rescue team.

There aren't any typical puzzles as in some other escape rooms that you can tell were separated from the theme. All the puzzles in Lunar Station make perfect sense, and more importantly, ALL fit the theme.

We were constantly surprised during this interactive journey by its game design, decoration, lighting and sounding effect, let alone the most awesome ending. From all the details, you can tell how much time and effort they put into this game. Thank you Maze Game, for bringing us such a great game.

We were told a new fairy theme one is under construction, and it will be even better than Lunar Station. We can't wait to come back!</review>

Been doing a lot of maze rooms and we were excited for the challenging Lunar escape.  Everything started out great, but about 1/2 through the room it became apparent that nothing was working the way it was supposed to.  The attendant kept having to manually push the room through to the next phase negating doing several puzzles.  When I tried to get some clarification on the things that were not working it was clear they did not want to deal with it.  Some of the puzzles seemed quite cool but really it was a small room that would be best for 2 - 3 players at most.
The way the puzzles are setup it doesn't allow a lot of people to work together on them.  With the way they handled my complaints (first time I've ever had any) I won't be going to any more Maze Rooms.< /review>

< text>
Came at around 4:00 for an early dinner. We ordered the smash burger and the chicken sandwich, both were delicious. I was surprised at how reasonable the prices were. Similar burger places would easily charge an extra 2-3 dollars for a comparable dish.
We also came with our puppy and sat out in the patio. I was surprised to find they offer puppy patties (plain hamburger patty) for four-legged friends.

The line did get long as we were leaving around 4:45 or so. I'd suggest coming in early if you don't want to wait in line to order.</text>

< Review>
It's a small local eatery in a shopping mall. To be honest, it kinda resembles Dog Haus  Biergarten but they do BBQ no hotdogs. They offer beer and wine. You order at counter, pick up beer at end and they bring you your food. I ordered the texas beef brisket grilled cheese. I liked the brisket, it was tender and flavorful. The grilled crunchy cheese was a plus. It was pretty good. My buddy ordered the Nashville hot chicken and Lauren's salad. The chicken sandwich had a good kick to it. Pretty spicy. The chicken tenders used where a little dry but it had a good crunch. I had to dip in some ranch to wet it. So, they have a secret menu. I only found out because a buddy sent me a post from Instagram and I asked a waitress if they had the sandwich. So it's a monster sandwich called the Mc Rib. It has a thick Rib bone, on top of their Texas beef brisket grilled cheese, on top of a double cheese burger. It was a monster. Least to say if could feed 3 or 4 small people. It did cost $30, but I needed to see and taste this monster. So the rib was thick and juicy. It had a good sauce glazed on. The brisket was the same and the burger just added a layer. It was difficult to choose which bite I wanted. It was so massive that you cant get a taste of everything in one bite. It was a fun food experience. I would say, try it once and its big enough to share the experience with a couple friends or family. I recommend the place, they have good BBQ. I gave them one less star mainly because the staff at the register didn't mention the secret menu when I asked about the food and specials.</Review>

<Rate>4< /Rate>< text>
Food was good, but service was excellent.

There are strict COVID safety measures in place, limiting the number of people who are allowed to queue to place an order. Patio dining is really well done with heat lamps/lights, and TV showing sports. Tables are distanced appropriately far enough to feel safe.

We did two orders and on both occasions we received "on the house" sides or a dessert. Makes you feel special! Also, very attentive service after the food is delivered when they come and check up on your table multiple times. If you have a dog, you'll also get a doggy treat "on the house".

Plenty of parking in the lot.</text>

< text>
My boyfriend Jorge and I went around lunch time and had the pleasure of meeting Tommy and Daisy at the front counter. The staff is out of control, they're so friendly and energetic and the customer service was refreshing.
We dined in at S&F and went full experience.
We ordered the Mac Rib and Hot Chicken Sandwich (medium heat) and were able to try a chicken strip(hot) and the mac and cheese ü•™

If you want to be able to just taste and enjoy the flavor I recommend medium heat, hot heat was a little too much for me but to each their own. The chicken sandwich was delicious and the texture of the crispiness was unique, it was crunchy but delicate, not like an over breaded tennessee hot chicken we are all probably used to. I loved the chicken itself and with the combination of the slaw and pickles it was flavorful and refreshing!

Man oh man! The crown jewel here is the brisket, the Mac Rib is a hefty piece of juicy meat cooked to perfection and we will DEFINITELY BE BACK FOR MORE BRISKET.

I want to try all the brisket dishes, they're so tender and juicy and melt in your mouth.

Thanks for having us, be back soon! üíï< /text>

We were finally able to make it out there on a Saturday. Like most places these days there is a line outside due to Covid. I have to give credit where its due, their line was moving along fast. I think there was 30 people or so, in front of us when we got in line. Took about 20 minutes to get to the register and place our order. Great organization of a line to get you in and out so you are not waiting long.

Now for the reason I only gave it 2 stars. Like most of you you probably want to try the delicious looking version of the McRib. Get to the register and they inform us that they are sold out of the McRib. Why not put a sign out front that says they are sold out so people can decided if they still want to wait in line or not. We brushed it off and decided to they their Smash burger, pretzel, and criss cross fries. Criss cross fries amazing, Smash burger was OK nothing special just a regular smash burger. Their pretzel and cheese was such a disappointment. The pretzel was cold and chewy, the cheese they give you for the pretzel was cold and the amount they gave you was very little. You are left with half a cold chewy pretzel when you are done with your cheese.

In conclusion: My tip for you guys that want to try the McRib. Go in and ask if they are sold out of the McRib before you wait in line . You want a pretzel with cheese? Ask for double cheese and have them warm it up before they bring it out to you.

P.S. They have some awesome art üòÅ</text>

< Review>
Came here for my birthday so that my non-vegan family also had something to enjoy. I got the stacked veg sando and a side of waffle fries. The outdoor patio was really pretty and also comfortable. We went in the evening. It was chilly but there were heaters available.

Oh boy I did not expect the vegan sando to be so so good. The oyster mushrooms were so meaty and crispy. The sandwich itself was packed with flavor and stacked to the top! So good! Overall really impressed with my meal.

I just wish there were more vegan options, I bet they would taste just as well as the sando. After eating the sando, I want to know what other vegan options they can come up with :-)<//Review>

<text>Casual setting, restaurant quality food. Order at the front, pick up towards the back by the soda fountain. The fries are big enough to split between 2 people. The chicken sandwich is solid and on the pricey side, $11.99. You're paying for an oversized chicken patty: crispy, moist and has some slow burn heat to it. The magic doesn't happen until you combine the slaw, chicken and bun. I would have loved a large bun to match the chicken patty with an equally larger spread of slaw. The smash burger is a no nonsense burger: crispy and seasoned to perfection. Usually you don't expect staff to check in on you when you order up front. They came by just after we got our food, once in between and at the end to bring us boxes. This must be Chick Fill A premium. My stomach wasn't big enough to try everyone on one go. Will definitely be back! <date>1619655069622</date>< Rating>
5</Rating>
< Text>
First time at this establishment and definitely won't be my last. Ordered the Mac Rib, a smash burger (cut in half to share), and some Nashville Hot Chicken Fries (for the table to share). Everything was delicious. The brisket was flavorful so next time I go I'll probably just order the Stockberger to get more of that amazing brisket. The Smash burger was nice and juicy. Fries ended up getting a little cold since we were indulging on the other items but still delicious nonetheless.

The icing on the cake at this establishment was one of the staff members by the name of Cailyn. She certainly knows the meaning of customer service. She's extremely observant. Once you order you sit at your table in the patio and wait for the staff to bring out your order. She noticed that we were sitting there a couple of minutes without our number being called. She then asked me what my order number was and proceeded to go check what was taking so long. She came back within seconds with our order. After that she came back a couple of times to see how we were doing and to ask if we needed anything. She was doing all this as she was constantly bringing out orders non-stop. To simply have the wherewithal to make sure we were good is the sign of someone that will quickly be ascending into management at this establishment. Customer service is such a huge component of the food service industry and Cailyn has it down pat. Looking forward to our next visit and hope Cailyn will be on staff that day.</Text>

<date>1604283332323</date><rate>5< /rate>< Review>
They deserve more then 5 stars! They hit the marks on all categories - friendliness of the staff, cleanliness of the place, and obviously the food. On top of that they serve halal meat! Great to see a top place serving quality food with halal meat.
Me and my brother went in and were greeted by one of the owners who was very friendly. Gave us an overview of the menu and also mentioned that their online menu has some secret items not listed in the store menu. One item he suggested to try was the brisket tacos. We then went to Tommy who is also a co owner and he was also amazing. Very friendly and he hooked us up. We ordered the brisket tacos, smash burger and he gave us chicken fries on the house!

We sat at the table and food didnt take long. Everything we ordered taste amazing!! These guys know how to cook. Their staff are very attentative and polite. They come every so often to see to check up in you or if we need something.

As for the food- the brisket melts in your mouth. The friend chicken with fries taste amazing. We asked him to make it spicy. It has a nice kick to it. And the smash burger was awesome.

This was place had a lot of good reviews so we went in with high expectations and to our surprise it did not dissapoint. I typically do not write long reviews but these guys know what they are doing.

I hope they can open some locations on the east coast where i am from! We meed more places like this that serve quality halal items.<//Review>

< review>
I was disappointed to receive a Smoke & Fire email titled 'WE ARE STAYING OPEN FOR PATIO DINE-IN! HAPPY HOLIDAYS'. On Smoke & Fire's website they describe themselves with the following: 'we see ourselves as more than a restaurant; our mission is to be a cornerstone in the community'.

While I empathize with small businesses navigating COVID restrictions, it is duplicitous for Smoke & Fire to state their explicit intent to defy state law and endanger the community they claim to desire to be a cornerstone of. Flouting temporary restrictions will only prolong the amount of time the county stays under 15% available ICU capacity and prevent those who are actually following the law from being able to offer patio and outdoor dining.

As for the food, it's overpriced and rather disappointing.<//review>

< Review>
Don't have any photos to post because I ate all the food before I could write this review. But I must say that this place goes above and beyond in both their food and service despite the COVID-19. I got the Nashville Hot Chicken sandwich (Mild) and my buddy got the Grilled Cheese Brisket sandwich with the waffle fries. The seasoning on the chicken with the coleslaw was so good! The waffle cut fries was crispy and soft on the inside! We also tried the brisket tacos and I gotta say I haven't had good brisket since I went to Texas...it was that good. The smoke ring and the tenderness was amazing on the brisket was just perfect and it shows the time and care the staff took into preparing everything on the menu. The smash burger was cooked perfectly and the umami from the maillard reaction from the meat and the melted cheese on the burger was just on point. Grab your masks and come eat here as there is also a dine-in for both indoor and outdoor! Thank you Juan and your team for the hospitality!< /Review>
